    display: inline;

  }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

          width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





this is a report to a security vulnerability in google chrome/chromium browser as high-quality report with functional exploit. this vulnerability allows attackers to steal thecache of input fields like usernames, e-mail adresses, telephone numbers from any site like twitter, google and any others (Chrome Autofill Saved Data).



<span class="line"><!---->this is a report to a security vulnerability in google chrome/chromium browser as high-quality report with functional exploit. this vulnerability allows attackers to steal thecache of input fields like usernames, e-mail adresses, telephone numbers from any site like twitter, google and any others (Chrome Autofill Saved Data).<!----></span>



<br>





-------------



<span class="line"><!---->-------------<!----></span>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Exploit tested with the following properties:



<span class="line"><!---->Exploit tested with the following properties:<!----></span>



<br>





Google Chrome (windows 10) Version 105.0.5195.54 (Official Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome (windows 10) Version 105.0.5195.54 (Official Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>



<br>





-----------



<span class="line"><!---->-----------<!----></span>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





the exploit use a vulnerability in showing of cache of input fields. your browser suggests the saved entries of input fields like saved user logins (username, email, phone number...) or cached search word any similar entered things.



<span class="line"><!---->the exploit use a vulnerability in showing of cache of input fields. your browser suggests the saved entries of input fields like saved user logins (username, email, phone number...) or cached search word any similar entered things.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





nobody will send critical information to unknown sites. but this can be hide by full bypassing the visibility of all fields and suggests. in this case nobody are able to notice that they are sending their data to unknown attackers.



<span class="line"><!---->nobody will send critical information to unknown sites. but this can be hide by full bypassing the visibility of all fields and suggests. in this case nobody are able to notice that they are sending their data to unknown attackers.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION STEPS



<span class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION STEPS<!----></span>



<br>





-------------------



<span class="line"><!---->-------------------<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





(Play a little jump and run game (Dino) to get hijacked any cached input of fieldname "username",email,telphone,address,cardnumber,.....)



<span class="line"><!---->(Play a little jump and run game (Dino) to get hijacked any cached input of fieldname "username",email,telphone,address,cardnumber,.....)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





**Before Repro you can add some data under chrome://settings/addresses and add some records



<span class="line"><!---->**Before Repro you can add some data under chrome://settings/addresses and add some records<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1-visit 



<span class="line"><!---->1-visit <!----></span>





https://vrphunt.com/chrome/canvasautofillwindows.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://vrphunt.com/chrome/canvasautofillwindows.html"><!---->https://vrphunt.com/chrome/canvasautofillwindows.html<!----></a>





 in  (Close and open page again If Start Button not correctly Shown/disabled)



<span class="line"><!----> in  (Close and open page again If Start Button not correctly Shown/disabled)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





2- Double click the button to start Game



<span class="line"><!---->2- Double click the button to start Game<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





3-Press Arrow UP/Down then Enter 



<span class="line"><!---->3-Press Arrow UP/Down then Enter <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Autofill data Will be shown in the Green Box 



<span class="line"><!---->Autofill data Will be shown in the Green Box <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





-------------



<span class="line"><!---->-------------<!----></span>

Thanks for the report. I'm redirecting to the AutoFill folks because I don't properly understand their threat model. 



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for the report. I'm redirecting to the AutoFill folks because I don't properly understand their threat model. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





There was a bug in the POC such that the contents of spoofautofillpop.html were visible, which was actually instructive for understanding how the attack works. Namely it attempts to trick the user to interact with a hidden form, luring key presses to cycle through auto-complete values. 



<span class="line"><!---->There was a bug in the POC such that the contents of spoofautofillpop.html were visible, which was actually instructive for understanding how the attack works. Namely it attempts to trick the user to interact with a hidden form, luring key presses to cycle through auto-complete values. <!----></span>

Hide Autofill popup if it overlaps with picture-in-picture window



<span class="line"><!---->Hide Autofill popup if it overlaps with picture-in-picture window<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL introduces BoundsOverlapWithPictureInPictureWindow used in



<span class="line"><!---->This CL introduces BoundsOverlapWithPictureInPictureWindow used in<!----></span>



<br>





autofill_popup_view_native_views.cc to determine whether there is an



<span class="line"><!---->autofill_popup_view_native_views.cc to determine whether there is an<!----></span>



<br>





overlap between the picture-in-picture window and the autofill popup.



<span class="line"><!---->overlap between the picture-in-picture window and the autofill popup.<!----></span>



<br>





If it does, it hides the autofill popup.



<span class="line"><!---->If it does, it hides the autofill popup.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Hide Autofill popup if it overlaps with picture-in-picture window



<span class="line"><!---->Hide Autofill popup if it overlaps with picture-in-picture window<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL introduces BoundsOverlapWithPictureInPictureWindow used in



<span class="line"><!---->This CL introduces BoundsOverlapWithPictureInPictureWindow used in<!----></span>



<br>





autofill_popup_view_native_views.cc to determine whether there is an



<span class="line"><!---->autofill_popup_view_native_views.cc to determine whether there is an<!----></span>



<br>





overlap between the picture-in-picture window and the autofill popup.



<span class="line"><!---->overlap between the picture-in-picture window and the autofill popup.<!----></span>



<br>





If it does, it hides the autofill popup.



<span class="line"><!---->If it does, it hides the autofill popup.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Hello, thank for your reaching out about this. There is no need for RV-SE or RV-G in this case, and actually these labels would be detrimental in this case as it would prohibit the Edge folk at MSFT and other embedders from accessing this fix. Once this issue was marked as Fixed it provided access to this issue and the fix to be leveraged in Edge and other Chromium based browsers and software at that time.

I thought it might be helpful to convey this is a standard process, and is exhibited by the Restrict-View-SecurityNotify label that is present on this bug, added just after it was updated as Fixed. This is the process that allows the Chromium embedders, like Edge and other Chromium-based browsers and software, to have access to the issue and see the related fix. MSFT folks and others already have access to this issue so no need to add any here and we certainly do not want to RV access away from them.



<span class="line"><!---->I thought it might be helpful to convey this is a standard process, and is exhibited by the Restrict-View-SecurityNotify label that is present on this bug, added just after it was updated as Fixed. This is the process that allows the Chromium embedders, like Edge and other Chromium-based browsers and software, to have access to the issue and see the related fix. MSFT folks and others already have access to this issue so no need to add any here and we certainly do not want to RV access away from them.<!----></span>

What MSFT is conveying is correct, because Chromium the upstream project that supports Edge. This issue lives in core Chromium, impacting Chrome and Edge, so the issue is in upstream. Google (Chrome Security team) are the stewards of Chromium security issues so this issue belongs does belong to Google who resolved it (well, specifically vidhanj@ resolved it). 



<span class="line"><!---->What MSFT is conveying is correct, because Chromium the upstream project that supports Edge. This issue lives in core Chromium, impacting Chrome and Edge, so the issue is in upstream. Google (Chrome Security team) are the stewards of Chromium security issues so this issue belongs does belong to Google who resolved it (well, specifically vidhanj@ resolved it). <!----></span>



<br>





As we fixed it, the fix is now (has been) available by downstream Chromium-based browsers, like Edge, and other Chromium based produced to be picked up and used in their updates of their products. 



<span class="line"><!---->As we fixed it, the fix is now (has been) available by downstream Chromium-based browsers, like Edge, and other Chromium based produced to be picked up and used in their updates of their products. <!----></span>



<br>





Hope this helps.



<span class="line"><!---->Hope this helps.<!----></span>
